(*****************************************************************************

 Orthogonality

 In this file, we define the left and right lifting properties of 1-cells in
 bicategories.

 The context in which we are interested in this notion, is given by orthogonal
 factorization system. In such a factorization, we have two classes of
 morphisms, which we call `L` and `R`. Each 1-cell in the bicategory can be
 factorized as `f · g` where `f` is in `L` and where `g` is in `R`. To
 guarantee that this factorization is unique up to unique invertible 2-cell,
 we require that a lifting property between maps in `L` and maps in `R`.
 This lifting property is expressed via orthogonal morphisms.

 Suppose that we have 1-cells `f : b₁ --> b₂` and `g` : c₁ --> c₂`. Then we
 say that `f` is left orthogonal to `g` (which we write as `f ⊥ g`) if the
 following diagrams is a weak pullback of categories:

<<
       B(b₂, c₁) -------------> B(b₁, c₁)
           |                        |
           |                        |
           V                        V
       B(b₂, c₂) -------------> B(b₁, c₂)
>>

 The maps are given as follows:
 - `B(b₂, c₁) --> B(b₁, c₁)`: precomposition with `f`
 - `B(b₂, c₁) --> B(b₂, c₂)`: postcomposition with `g`
 - `B(b₂, c₂) --> B(b₁, c₂)`: precomposition with `f`
 - `B(b₁, c₁) --> B(b₁, c₂)`: postcomposition with `g`

 Note that weak pullbacks of categories are given by iso-comma categories. We
 express this lifting property by saying that a certain functor is an adjoint
 equivalence of categories ([orthogonal]). This functor ([orthogonal_functor])
 has type: `hom b₂ c₁ ⟶ iso_comma (post_comp b₁ g) (pre_comp c₂ f)`, so it
 is the functor that we obtain from the universal property of the iso-comma
 category.

 To verify whether two classes of morphisms are orthogonal, one needs to
 establish that a certain functor is an equivalence. To do so, it suffices to
 check that this functor is essentially surjective and fully faithful (assuming
 that the bicategory is locally univalent. Each of these properties has a
 rather natural interpretation.
 - Essential surjectivity ([orthogonal_essentially_surjective]): if we are given
   a square as follows

<<
       b₁ ------------> c₁
       |                |
     f |                | g
       |                |
       V                V
       b₂ ------------> c₂
>>

   where `f` is in the left class and where `g` is in the right class, then
   we can find a lift `l : b₂ --> c₁` such that the resulting triangle commute
   up to invertible 2-cell (and some coherence condition).
 - Fullness ([orthogonal_full]): if we are given two lifts `l₁, l₂ : b₂ --> c₁`,
   then we can obtain a 2-cell `l₁ ==> l₂` if we have 2-cells `f · l₁ ==> f · l₂`
   and `l₁ · g ==> l₂ · g` (again requiring some coherence condition)
 - Faithfulness ([orthogonal_faithful]) expresses the uniqueness of the 2-cell
   obtained from fullness.

 Finally, we show that the definition in this file, is equivalent to definition
 of orthogonality expressed via pullbacks.

 Contents
 1. Orthogonality
 2. Constructing orthogonal morphisms
 3. Projections of orthogonal morphisms
 3.1. Lifting property for for 1-cells
 3.2. Lifting property for for 2-cells
 3.3. Lifting property for for equalities
 4. Orthogonality via pullbacks
 5. Equivalence of the definitions

 *****************************************************************************)

(** * 1. Orthogonality *)

B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
hom b₂ c₁ ⟶ iso_comma (post_comp b₁ g) (pre_comp c₂ f)


B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
hom b₂ c₁ ⟶ iso_comma (post_comp b₁ g) (pre_comp c₂ f)

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
hom b₂ c₁ ⟶ hom b₁ c₁
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
hom b₂ c₁ ⟶ hom b₂ c₂
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
nat_z_iso (?P ∙ post_comp b₁ g) (?Q ∙ pre_comp c₂ f)

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
hom b₂ c₁ ⟶ hom b₁ c₁
 exact (pre_comp c₁ f).
  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
hom b₂ c₁ ⟶ hom b₂ c₂
 exact (post_comp b₂ g).
  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
c₁, c₂: B
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
nat_z_iso (pre_comp c₁ f ∙ post_comp b₁ g)
  (post_comp b₂ g ∙ pre_comp c₂ f)
 exact (pre_comp_post_comp_commute_z_iso f g).
Defined.

Definition orthogonal
           {B : bicat}
           {b₁ b₂ c₁ c₂ : B}
           (f : b₁ --> b₂)
           (g : c₁ --> c₂)
  : UU
  := adj_equivalence_of_cats (orthogonal_functor f g).

Notation "f ⊥ g" := (orthogonal f g) (at level 60) : cat.


B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
HB_2_1: is_univalent_2_1 B
isaprop (f ⊥ g)


B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
HB_2_1: is_univalent_2_1 B
isaprop (f ⊥ g)

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
HB_2_1: is_univalent_2_1 B
isofhlevel 1
  (Adjunctions.left_adjoint_equivalence
     (orthogonal_functor f g))

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
HB_2_1: is_univalent_2_1 B
is_univalent_2_1 bicat_of_univ_cats

  exact univalent_cat_is_univalent_2_1.
Qed.

(** * 2. Constructing orthogonal morphisms *)
Section ConstructOrthogonality.
  Context {B : bicat}
          {b₁ b₂ c₁ c₂ : B}
          (f : b₁ --> b₂)
          (g : c₁ --> c₂).

  Definition orthogonal_essentially_surjective
    : UU
    := ∏ (φ₁ : b₁ --> c₁)
         (φ₂ : b₂ --> c₂)
         (α : invertible_2cell (φ₁ · g) (f · φ₂)),
       ∑ (l : b₂ --> c₁)
         (ζ₁ : invertible_2cell (f · l) φ₁)
         (ζ₂ : invertible_2cell (l · g) φ₂),
       (ζ₁ ▹ g) • α = rassociator _ _ _ • (f ◃ ζ₂).

  Definition orthogonal_full
    : UU
    := ∏ (l₁ l₂ : b₂ --> c₁)
         (k₁ : f · l₁ ==> f · l₂)
         (k₂ : l₁ · g ==> l₂ · g)
         (p : (k₁ ▹ g) • rassociator _ _ _
              =
              rassociator _ _ _ • (f ◃ k₂)),
       ∑ (ξ : l₁ ==> l₂),
       f ◃ ξ = k₁
       ×
       ξ ▹ g = k₂.

  Definition orthogonal_faithful
    : UU
    := ∏ (l₁ l₂ : b₂ --> c₁)
         (ζ₁ ζ₂ : l₁ ==> l₂),
       f ◃ ζ₁ = f ◃ ζ₂
       →
       ζ₁ ▹ g = ζ₂ ▹ g
       →
       ζ₁ = ζ₂.

  Section MakeOrthogonal.
    Context (HB_2_1 : is_univalent_2_1 B)
            (H₁ : orthogonal_full)
            (H₂ : orthogonal_faithful)
            (H₃ : orthogonal_essentially_surjective).

    
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
HB_2_1: is_univalent_2_1 B
H₁: orthogonal_full
H₂: orthogonal_faithful
H₃: orthogonal_essentially_surjective
full (orthogonal_functor f g)

    
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
HB_2_1: is_univalent_2_1 B
H₁: orthogonal_full
H₂: orthogonal_faithful
H₃: orthogonal_essentially_surjective
full (orthogonal_functor f g)

      
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧

H₁: orthogonal_full
H₂: orthogonal_faithful
H₃: orthogonal_essentially_surjective
l₁, l₂: hom b₂ c₁
issurjective
  (λ f0 : hom b₂ c₁ ⟦ l₁, l₂ ⟧,
   # (orthogonal_functor f g) f0)

    (λ f0 : hom b₂ c₁ ⟦ l₁, l₂ ⟧,
     # (orthogonal_functor f g) f0) k ∥

   # (orthogonal_functor f g) f0) k

b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B

l₁ ==> l₂

(ζ₁ ▹ g) • z_iso_to_inv2cell (pr2 h) =
rassociator f l g • (f ◃ ζ₂)
pr1 ℓ · g ==> pr21 h
 exact (pr122 ℓ).
          
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
HB_2_1: is_univalent_2_1 B
H₁: orthogonal_full
H₂: orthogonal_faithful
H₃: orthogonal_essentially_surjective
h: iso_comma (post_comp b₁ g) (pre_comp c₂ f)
ℓ:= H₃ (pr11 h) (pr21 h) (z_iso_to_inv2cell (pr2 h)): ∑ (l : B ⟦ b₂, c₁ ⟧)
(ζ₁ : invertible_2cell (f · l) (pr11 h))
(ζ₂ : invertible_2cell (l · g) (pr21 h)),
(ζ₁ ▹ g) • z_iso_to_inv2cell (pr2 h) =
rassociator f l g • (f ◃ ζ₂)
(pr12 ℓ ▹ g) • pr2 h =
rassociator f (pr1 ℓ) g • (f ◃ pr122 ℓ)
 exact (pr222 ℓ).
        
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
HB_2_1: is_univalent_2_1 B
H₁: orthogonal_full
H₂: orthogonal_faithful
H₃: orthogonal_essentially_surjective
h: iso_comma (post_comp b₁ g) (pre_comp c₂ f)
ℓ:= H₃ (pr11 h) (pr21 h) (z_iso_to_inv2cell (pr2 h)): ∑ (l : B ⟦ b₂, c₁ ⟧)
(ζ₁ : invertible_2cell (f · l) (pr11 h))
(ζ₂ : invertible_2cell (l · g) (pr21 h)),
(ζ₁ ▹ g) • z_iso_to_inv2cell (pr2 h) =
rassociator f l g • (f ◃ ζ₂)
is_z_isomorphism
  (((pr12 ℓ
     :
     hom b₁ c₁
     ⟦ pr11 (orthogonal_functor f g (pr1 ℓ)), pr11 h ⟧),,
    (pr122 ℓ
     :
     (λ _ : hom b₁ c₁
            ⟦ pr11 (orthogonal_functor f g (pr1 ℓ)),
            pr11 h ⟧,
      hom b₂ c₂
      ⟦ pr21 (orthogonal_functor f g (pr1 ℓ)), pr21 h
      ⟧)
       (pr12 ℓ
        :
        hom b₁ c₁
        ⟦ pr11 (orthogonal_functor f g (pr1 ℓ)),
        pr11 h ⟧))),,
   (pr222 ℓ
    :
    (λ f0 : PrecategoryBinProduct.category_binproduct
              (hom b₁ c₁) (hom b₂ c₂)
            ⟦ pr1 (orthogonal_functor f g (pr1 ℓ)),
            pr1 h ⟧,
     Core.mor_disp
       (pr2 (orthogonal_functor f g (pr1 ℓ))) (pr2 h)
       f0)
      ((pr12 ℓ
        :
        hom b₁ c₁
        ⟦ pr11 (orthogonal_functor f g (pr1 ℓ)),
        pr11 h ⟧),,
       (pr122 ℓ
        :
        (λ _ : hom b₁ c₁
               ⟦ pr11 (orthogonal_functor f g (pr1 ℓ)),
               pr11 h ⟧,
         hom b₂ c₂
         ⟦ pr21 (orthogonal_functor f g (pr1 ℓ)),
         pr21 h ⟧)
          (pr12 ℓ
           :
           hom b₁ c₁
           ⟦ pr11 (orthogonal_functor f g (pr1 ℓ)),
           pr11 h ⟧)))))

                (pr12 ℓ
                 :

                 ⟦ pr11 (orthogonal_functor f g
                           (pr1 ℓ)), pr11 h ⟧))))))

        exact HB_2_1.
      
B: bicat

    Defined.
  End MakeOrthogonal.
End ConstructOrthogonality.

(** * 3. Projections of orthogonal morphisms *)
Section OrthogonalityProjections.
  Context {B : bicat}
          {b₁ b₂ c₁ c₂ : B}
          {f : b₁ --> b₂}
          {g : c₁ --> c₂}
          (H : f ⊥ g).

  (** ** 3.1. Lifting property for for 1-cells *)
  Section LiftOne.
    Context (φ₁ : b₁ --> c₁)
            (φ₂ : b₂ --> c₂)
            (α : invertible_2cell (φ₁ · g) (f · φ₂)).

      Definition orthogonal_lift_1
        : b₂ --> c₁
        := right_adjoint (H : adj_equivalence_of_cats _) ((φ₁ ,, φ₂) ,, inv2cell_to_z_iso α).

      
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
H: f ⊥ g
φ₁: B ⟦ b₁, c₁ ⟧
φ₂: B ⟦ b₂, c₂ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell (φ₁ · g) (f · φ₂)
invertible_2cell (f · orthogonal_lift_1) φ₁

      
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
H: f ⊥ g
φ₁: B ⟦ b₁, c₁ ⟧
φ₂: B ⟦ b₂, c₂ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell (φ₁ · g) (f · φ₂)
invertible_2cell (f · orthogonal_lift_1) φ₁

        
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
H: f ⊥ g
φ₁: B ⟦ b₁, c₁ ⟧
φ₂: B ⟦ b₂, c₂ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell (φ₁ · g) (f · φ₂)
z_iso (f · orthogonal_lift_1) φ₁

        exact (functor_on_z_iso
                (iso_comma_pr1 _ _)
                (counit_pointwise_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence
                   H
                   ((φ₁ ,, φ₂) ,, inv2cell_to_z_iso α))).
      Defined.

      
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
H: f ⊥ g
φ₁: B ⟦ b₁, c₁ ⟧
φ₂: B ⟦ b₂, c₂ ⟧
α: invertible_2cell (φ₁ · g) (f · φ₂)
invertible_2cell (orthogonal_lift_1 · g) φ₂

      
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
H: f ⊥ g
φ₁: B ⟦ b₁, c₁ ⟧
φ₂: B ⟦ b₂, c₂ ⟧

invertible_2cell (orthogonal_lift_1 · g) φ₂

        
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
H: f ⊥ g

z_iso (orthogonal_lift_1 · g) φ₂

        exact (functor_on_z_iso
                 (iso_comma_pr2 _ _)
                 (counit_pointwise_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence
                    H
                    ((φ₁ ,, φ₂) ,, inv2cell_to_z_iso α))).
      Defined.

      Definition orthogonal_lift_1_eq
        : (orthogonal_lift_1_comm_left ▹ g) • α
          =
          rassociator _ _ _ • (f ◃ orthogonal_lift_1_comm_right)
        := pr2 (counit_from_left_adjoint
                  (pr1 H)
                  ((φ₁ ,, φ₂) ,, inv2cell_to_z_iso α)).
    End LiftOne.

    (** ** 3.2. Lifting property for for 2-cells *)
    Section LiftTwo.
      Context (l₁ l₂ : b₂ --> c₁)
              (k₁ : f · l₁ ==> f · l₂)
              (k₂ : l₁ · g ==> l₂ · g)
              (p : (k₁ ▹ g) • rassociator _ _ _
                   =
                   rassociator _ _ _ • (f ◃ k₂)).

      Let R : iso_comma (post_comp b₁ g) (pre_comp c₂ f) ⟶ hom b₂ c₁
        := right_adjoint (H : adj_equivalence_of_cats _).

      Let φ : iso_comma (post_comp b₁ g) (pre_comp c₂ f)
        := (f · l₁ ,, l₁ · g) ,, inv2cell_to_z_iso (rassociator_invertible_2cell _ _ _).
      Let ψ : iso_comma (post_comp b₁ g) (pre_comp c₂ f)
        := (f · l₂ ,, l₂ · g) ,, inv2cell_to_z_iso (rassociator_invertible_2cell _ _ _).
      Let μ : φ --> ψ
        := (k₁ ,, k₂) ,, p.

      Let η₁ : l₁ ==> R φ
        := unit_from_left_adjoint (H : adj_equivalence_of_cats _) l₁.
      Let η₂ : R ψ ==> l₂
        := (z_iso_to_inv2cell (unit_pointwise_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence H l₂))^-1.
      Let ε₁ : f · R φ ==> f · l₁
        := pr11 (counit_from_left_adjoint (pr1 H) φ).
      Let ε₂ : f · R ψ ==> f · l₂
        := pr11 (counit_from_left_adjoint (pr1 H) ψ).
      Let ε₁' : R φ · g ==> l₁ · g
        := pr21 (counit_from_left_adjoint (pr1 H) φ).
      Let ε₂' : R ψ · g ==> l₂ · g
        := pr21 (counit_from_left_adjoint (pr1 H) ψ).

      Definition orthogonal_lift_2
        : l₁ ==> l₂
        := η₁ • #R μ • η₂.

      
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
H: f ⊥ g
l₁, l₂: B ⟦ b₂, c₁ ⟧
k₁: f · l₁ ==> f · l₂
k₂: l₁ · g ==> l₂ · g
p: (k₁ ▹ g) • rassociator f l₂ g =
rassociator f l₁ g • (f ◃ k₂)
R:= right_adjoint
  (H
   :
   adj_equivalence_of_cats (orthogonal_functor f g)): iso_comma (post_comp b₁ g) (pre_comp c₂ f)
⟶ hom b₂ c₁
φ:= (f · l₁,, l₁ · g),,
inv2cell_to_z_iso
  (rassociator_invertible_2cell f l₁ g): iso_comma (post_comp b₁ g) (pre_comp c₂ f)
ψ:= (f · l₂,, l₂ · g),,
inv2cell_to_z_iso
  (rassociator_invertible_2cell f l₂ g): iso_comma (post_comp b₁ g) (pre_comp c₂ f)
μ:= (k₁,, k₂),, p: iso_comma (post_comp b₁ g) (pre_comp c₂ f) ⟦ φ, ψ
⟧
η₁:= unit_from_left_adjoint
  (H
   :
   adj_equivalence_of_cats
     (orthogonal_functor f g)) l₁: l₁ ==> R φ
η₂:= (z_iso_to_inv2cell
   (unit_pointwise_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence H l₂))
^-1: R ψ ==> l₂
ε₁:= pr11 (counit_from_left_adjoint (pr1 H) φ): f · R φ ==> f · l₁
ε₂:= pr11 (counit_from_left_adjoint (pr1 H) ψ): f · R ψ ==> f · l₂
ε₁':= pr21 (counit_from_left_adjoint (pr1 H) φ): R φ · g ==> l₁ · g
ε₂':= pr21 (counit_from_left_adjoint (pr1 H) ψ): R ψ · g ==> l₂ · g
is_invertible_2cell ε₂

      
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
H: f ⊥ g
l₁, l₂: B ⟦ b₂, c₁ ⟧
k₁: f · l₁ ==> f · l₂
k₂: l₁ · g ==> l₂ · g
p: (k₁ ▹ g) • rassociator f l₂ g =

  (rassociator_invertible_2cell f l₂ g): iso_comma (post_comp b₁ g) (pre_comp c₂ f)

  (H

is_invertible_2cell ε₂

        exact (property_from_invertible_2cell
                 (z_iso_to_inv2cell
                    (functor_on_z_iso
                       (iso_comma_pr1 _ _)
                       (counit_pointwise_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence H ψ)))).
      Qed.

ε₂':= pr21 (counit_from_left_adjoint (pr1 H) ψ): R ψ · g ==> l₂ · g
k₁ = k₁

        apply idpath.
      Qed.

g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
H: f ⊥ g
l₁, l₂: B ⟦ b₂, c₁ ⟧
k₁: f · l₁ ==> f · l₂
k₂: l₁ · g ==> l₂ · g
p: (k₁ ▹ g) • rassociator f l₂ g =
rassociator f l₁ g • (f ◃ k₂)
R:= right_adjoint
  (H
   :
   adj_equivalence_of_cats (orthogonal_functor f g)): iso_comma (post_comp b₁ g) (pre_comp c₂ f)
⟶ hom b₂ c₁
φ:= (f · l₁,, l₁ · g),,
inv2cell_to_z_iso
  (rassociator_invertible_2cell f l₁ g): iso_comma (post_comp b₁ g) (pre_comp c₂ f)
ψ:= (f · l₂,, l₂ · g),,
inv2cell_to_z_iso
  (rassociator_invertible_2cell f l₂ g): iso_comma (post_comp b₁ g) (pre_comp c₂ f)
μ:= (k₁,, k₂),, p: iso_comma (post_comp b₁ g) (pre_comp c₂ f) ⟦ φ, ψ
⟧
η₁:= unit_from_left_adjoint
  (H
   :
   adj_equivalence_of_cats
     (orthogonal_functor f g)) l₁: l₁ ==> R φ
η₂:= (z_iso_to_inv2cell
   (unit_pointwise_z_iso_from_adj_equivalence H l₂))
^-1: R ψ ==> l₂
ε₁:= pr11 (counit_from_left_adjoint (pr1 H) φ): f · R φ ==> f · l₁
ε₂:= pr11 (counit_from_left_adjoint (pr1 H) ψ): f · R ψ ==> f · l₂
ε₁':= pr21 (counit_from_left_adjoint (pr1 H) φ): R φ · g ==> l₁ · g
ε₂':= pr21 (counit_from_left_adjoint (pr1 H) ψ): R ψ · g ==> l₂ · g
?b =
k₂ • ((unit_from_are_adjoints (pr2 H) l₂ ▹ g) • ε₂')

f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
H: f ⊥ g
l₁, l₂: B ⟦ b₂, c₁ ⟧
ζ₁, ζ₂: l₁ ==> l₂
p₁: f ◃ ζ₁ = f ◃ ζ₂
p₂: ζ₁ ▹ g = ζ₂ ▹ g
Heq:= pr2
  (fully_faithful_implies_full_and_faithful
     (hom b₂ c₁)
     (iso_comma (post_comp b₁ g) (pre_comp c₂ f))
     (orthogonal_functor f g)
     (fully_faithful_from_equivalence (hom b₂ c₁)
        (iso_comma (post_comp b₁ g)
           (pre_comp c₂ f))
        (orthogonal_functor f g) H)) l₁ l₂: isincl (λ f0 : hom b₂ c₁ ⟦ l₁, l₂ ⟧, # (orthogonal_functor f g) f0)

rassociator f l₁ g • (f ◃ (ζ₁ ▹ g))
r₂: ((f ◃ ζ₂) ▹ g) • rassociator f l₂ g =
rassociator f l₁ g • (f ◃ (ζ₂ ▹ g))
ζ₁ = ζ₂

        (orthogonal_functor f g) H)) l₁ l₂: isincl (λ f0 : hom b₂ c₁ ⟦ l₁, l₂ ⟧, # (orthogonal_functor f g) f0)

rassociator f l₁ g • (f ◃ (ζ₁ ▹ g))
r₂: ((f ◃ ζ₂) ▹ g) • rassociator f l₂ g =
rassociator f l₁ g • (f ◃ (ζ₂ ▹ g))
Hprop:= proofirrelevance
  (hfiber
     (λ f0 : hom b₂ c₁ ⟦ l₁, l₂ ⟧,
      # (orthogonal_functor f g) f0)
     (((f ◃ ζ₁),, ζ₁ ▹ g),, r₁))
  (Heq (((f ◃ ζ₁),, ζ₁ ▹ g),, r₁)): isProofIrrelevant
  (hfiber
     (λ f0 : hom b₂ c₁ ⟦ l₁, l₂ ⟧,
      # (orthogonal_functor f g) f0)
     (((f ◃ ζ₁),, ζ₁ ▹ g),, r₁))
ζ₂ ▹ g = ζ₁ ▹ g
 exact (!p₂).
    Qed.
End OrthogonalityProjections.

Section OrthogonalityViaPullback.
  Context {B : bicat}
          {b₁ b₂ c₁ c₂ : B}
          (f : b₁ --> b₂)
          (g : c₁ --> c₂).

  (**
   4. Orthogonality via pullbacks
   *)
  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
HB_2_1: is_univalent_2_1 B
pb_cone (post_comp b₁ g) (pre_comp c₂ f)

  (?π₂ · pre_comp c₂ f)

nat_z_iso (pre_comp c₁ f · post_comp b₁ g)
  (post_comp b₂ g · pre_comp c₂ f)

      exact (pre_comp_post_comp_commute_z_iso f g).
  Defined.

  Definition orthogonal_via_pb
             (HB_2_1 : is_univalent_2_1 B)
    : UU
    := has_pb_ump (orthogonal_via_pb_cone HB_2_1).

        (pre_comp c₂ f))
     (orthogonal_via_pb_cone HB_2_1))
c: orthogonal_via_pb_cone HB_2_1
is_z_isomorphism
  (pr21 (pr1
           (orthogonal_via_pb_to_orthogonal_nat_trans
              HB_2_1) c))

      
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
HB_2_1: is_univalent_2_1 B
Hf: orthogonal_via_pb HB_2_1
p:= pb_ump_mor_left_adjoint_equivalence
  (iso_comma_pb_cone (post_comp b₁ g)
     (pre_comp c₂ f))
  (orthogonal_via_pb_cone HB_2_1)
  (iso_comma_has_pb_ump 
     (post_comp b₁ g) (pre_comp c₂ f)) Hf: Adjunctions.left_adjoint_equivalence
  (pb_ump_mor
     (iso_comma_has_pb_ump 
        (post_comp b₁ g) 
        (pre_comp c₂ f))
     (orthogonal_via_pb_cone HB_2_1))
c: orthogonal_via_pb_cone HB_2_1
is_z_isomorphism
  (pr11 (pr1
           (orthogonal_via_pb_to_orthogonal_nat_trans
              HB_2_1) c))

        is_iso.

f ⊥ g ≃ orthogonal_via_pb HB_2_1

isaprop (f ⊥ g)
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧

B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
HB_2_1: is_univalent_2_1 B
f ⊥ g → orthogonal_via_pb HB_2_1
 exact (orthogonal_to_orthogonal_via_pb HB_2_1).
    
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
HB_2_1: is_univalent_2_1 B
orthogonal_via_pb HB_2_1 → f ⊥ g
 exact (orthogonal_via_pb_to_orthogonal HB_2_1).
    
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
HB_2_1: is_univalent_2_1 B
isaprop (f ⊥ g)
 exact (isaprop_orthogonal f g HB_2_1).
    
B: bicat
b₁, b₂, c₁, c₂: B
f: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
g: B ⟦ c₁, c₂ ⟧
HB_2_1: is_univalent_2_1 B
isaprop (orthogonal_via_pb HB_2_1)
 exact (isaprop_orthogonal_via_pb HB_2_1).
  Defined.
